 How Doklam was negotiated between India and China in a secret manner
 padhie doklam main bharat kikootnithik vijay kii insaide story
 
 
 At first, China was not ready to negotiate on Doklam
 china kaa kahana tha ki pehle bharat sainik hataae, phir koi baatcheet ho sakati he
 India's position was that the troops would withdraw only after diplomatic negotiations on Doklam
 baatcheet kii shuruyaat tab hui jab rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar ajit dowaal china gaye the
 Ajit Doval met China's National Security Advisor during the BRICS meeting
 takaraav ke bich hi donon rashtriya suraksha salaahkaaron ke bich phone par baatcheet hoti rahi
 The controversy over Doklam was also expected to have an impact on the BRICS conference in China
 bharat ne tay nahin kiya tha ki pradhanmantri narendra modibrics deshon ke sammelan main china jaaenge yaa nahin
 It is believed that the condition of PM Modi's visit to China was put to resolve the dispute on Doklam
 isi bich china kii dhamkiyon ko jawaab dene ke liye bhartiya sena ne bhi seemaa par apni taiyaari kar lee thi
 The entire preparations of the Indian Army on the border put reverse pressure on the frightened China by talking of war
 china ko saaf pataa chal gaya tha ki yuddh kii dhamkiyon se doklam main bharat ko daraaya nahin ja saktaa

 rashtriya suraksha salaahkaar kaa china daura27 july ko ajit dowaal beijing gaye the, uske baad se baatcheet chal rahi thi
 On August 3, China admitted that negotiations were going on on Doklam
 china ne ye kaha tha ki baatcheet main bharat ne kuch sharten rakhi hai, jo maanane ke yogya nahin hai

 aakhirkaar doklam kaa hal niklaa to takaraav kii jagah se sainik hataane par sahmati hui

 baat ban gai he

 iske baad ballebaaji karne utre captain rohit (19) ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 23 ran hi jod sake the ki jadeja ne simons ko pawan negi ke haathon lapakvaa diya or super kings par bad rahe khatre ko taal diya
 Simmons meanwhile hit three fours and five sixes in his 51-ball fifty
 simons kaa ipel-8 main yah paanchvaan ardhashatak he tathaa iske saath hi vah mumbai indiens ke liye kisi ek sanskaran main sachin tendulkar or jepi dumini ke saath sanyukt rup se sarvaadhik ardhashatak lagane vaale ballebaaj ban gaye
 However, for Mumbai, who have scored 135 for two in 15 overs, the next two overs were quite poor
 in do overon main mumbai ne chah ran jodne main rohit or hardik pandya (1) ke wicket ganvaa die
 Bravo took the wicket of Rohit while Ashish Nehra took the wicket of Pandya
 krij par maujuud pollard ne haalanki tej haath dikhaate hue 17 gendon main ek chaukaa or paanch chakka jadkar team ko chunauteepurn score tak pahunchaa diya
 Meanwhile, Ambati Rayudu (10) fell victim to Mohit Sharma
 tippaniyan Pollard also played a very high ball from Bravo on the fourth ball of the last over and Suresh Raina made no mistake in taking the catch
 chennai ke liye braavo ne sarvaadhik teen wicket hasil kiye or iske saath hi ipel-8 main unke kul viketon kii sankhya 23 ho gai tathaa ipel-8 main vah sarvaadhik wicket lene vaale gendbaaj bane hue hai
 Faf du Plessis (45), who came to bat after this, kept the hopes of the team by sharing 46 runs for the second wicket with Michael Hussey (16) and 40 runs for the third wicket with Suresh Raina (25)
 hasi is bich vinay kumaar dwaara laae gaye chathe over kii pehali gend par wicket ke peeche lapak liye gaye
 Raina, Plessis, was engaged in trying to prove that Mumbai Indians experienced spin bowler Harbhajan Singh, who brought the 11th over, struck power on the hopes of Super Kings by taking the wickets of Raina and captain Mahendra Singh Dhoni (0) in two consecutive balls
 Dropped
 plasis ne haalanki ummid nahin chodi or dwen braavo (20) ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 24 ran jode
 Plessis, who was trying to increase the run pace, played Jagdisha Suchit's ball high on the leg side, however, Vinay Kumar, standing on the start, took the catch easily
 plasis ne 34 gendon kaa saamana kar paanch chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 Super Kings' troubles also started with Plessis leaving, and Bravo and Pawan Negi (3) also returned to the pavilion in the next two overs
 teji se doosraa ran lene kii koshish kar rahe braavo ko wicketiper parthiv patel ne sujh or phurti se ran out kiya
 Negi was caught at the hands of Vinay Kumar off substitute fielder Unmukt Chand
 is bich super kings ke liye apekshit ran gati badhati ja rahi thi or unhen aakhri chaar overon main jeet ke liye 59 ranon kii darkaar thi
 Although Ravichandran Ashwin (23) and Ravindra Jadeja (19) may not have raised hopes of winning by putting some quick shots, but kept the match exciting
 jadeja ne 10 gend main ek chaukaa or ek chakka jadaa, jabaki aswin ne 12 gendon main do chaukaa or ek chakka lagaaya
 However, despite all the efforts, the entire team of Super Kings returned to the pavilion for 162 runs an over
 mumbai ke liye malinga ne sarvaadhik teen, jabaki vinay kumaar or harbhajan ne do-do wicket chatkaaye
 Malinga was the most economical bowler
 isse pehle, mumbai ne landal simons (65) or kirone pollard (41) kii shandaar pariyon kii badaulat nirdhaarit 20 overon main chah wicket khokar 187 ranon kaa chunauteepurn score khadaa kiya
 Captain Rohit Sharma won the toss and decided to bat and both of his openers Simmons and Parthiv Patel (35) gave the team a brilliant start, citing their captain's fearless playing statement
 simons ne patel ke saath pehle wicket ke liye 10
 Add 90 runs in 4 overs
 apane sabhi spin gendbaajon ko aajamaa chuke captain dhoni ne antat: aakhri ke overon ke pasandida gendbaaj dwen braavo ko 11wein over main akraman par lagaaya
 Bravo catches Patel at the hands of Ravindra Jadeja and finally gives Super Kings the first success
 patel ne 25 gendon main chaar chauke or ek chakka lagaaya
 After that, with the captain Rohit (19), who came out to bat, he could add 23 runs for the second wicket that Jadeja caught Simmons at the hands of Pawan Negi and defended the growing threat on the Super Kings
 simons ne is bich 51 gendon kii apni ardhashtakeey pari main teen chauke or paanch chakke lagaae
 This is Simmons' fifth half-century in IPL-8, making him the joint batsman for Mumbai Indians with Sachin Tendulkar and JP Duminy for the most fifties in any one edition
 15 overon main do wicket par 135 ran bana chuki mumbai ke liye haalanki agle do over kaaphi kharaab rahe
 In these two overs, Mumbai lost the wickets of Rohit and Hardik Pandya (1) in adding six runs
 rohit kaa wicket braavo ne jabaki pandya kaa wicket ashish nehra ne liya
 Pollard, who was present at the crease, though showing a sharp hand, hit a four and a six in 17 balls to give the team a challenging score
 is bich ambati rayudu (10) mohit sharma kaa shikaar hue
 The comments pollard bhi aakhri over kii chauthi gend par braavo kii gend ko kaaphi ooncha khel baithe or suresh raina ne kaich lene main koi galati nahin kii
 Bravo grabbed the highest three wickets for Chennai and with this, his total wickets in the IPL-8 has gone up to 23 and he remains the highest wicket-taker in the IPL-8
 hasi is bich vinay kumaar dwaara laae gaye chathe over kii pehali gend par wicket ke peeche lapak liye gaye

 raina, plasis kii jodi sadhane kii koshishon main hi lagi hui thi ki 11waan over lekar aae mumbai indiens ke anbhavi spin gendbaaj harbhajan singh ne lagaataar do gendon par raina or captain mahendra singh dhoni (0) ke wicket chatka kar super kings kii ummiido par bijli gira di
 Plessis, however, did not give up hope and added 24 runs for the fifth wicket with Dwayne Bravo (20)
 ran gati badhaane kii koshishon main lage plasis ne jagadisha suchit kii gend ko leg said main ooncha khelaa haalanki long on par khadey vinay kumaar ne yah kaich aasaani se le liya
 Plessis faced 34 balls with five fours and a six
 plasis ke jate hi super kings kii museebataan bhi shuru ho gayi or agle do overon main braavo or pawan negi (3) bhi pavilion laut gaye
 Bravo, who was trying to take a quick second run, was run out by wicketkeeper Parthiv Patel from Sujh and Furti
 negi, vinay kumaar kii gend par sthanapann kshetrarakshak unmukt chand ke haathon lapke gaye
 In the meantime, the expected run pace for the Super Kings was increasing and they needed 59 runs to win the last four overs
 haalanki ravichandran aswin (23) or rabindra jadeja (19) ne kuch tej shot lagaakar jeet kii ummid bhale na jagaai ho, lekin match ko romaanchak banaae rakhaa
 Jadeja hit a four and a six in 10 balls, while Ashwin hit two fours and a six in 12 balls
 haalanki sari koshishon ke baavjood super kings kii puri team ek over pehle hi 162 ranon par pavilion laut gai
 Malinga top-scored for Mumbai with three, while Vinay Kumar and Harbhajan took two wickets each
 malinga ne sabase kifayati gendbaaj rahe
 Earlier, Mumbai scored a challenging total of 187 runs losing six wickets in 20 overs thanks to superb innings by Lendl Simmons (65) and Kieron Pollard (41)
 captain rohit sharma ne toss jitkar ballebaaji kaa faisla kiya or unke donon salaami ballebaajon simons or parthiv patel (35) ne apane captain ke nidar hokar khilne vaale bayaan ko charitaarth karte hue team ko shandaar shuruyaat dilaai
 Simmons scored 10 for the first wicket with Patel
 4 overon main 90 ran jod daale
